name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Parent-child Room

info:Family
info:12 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 21, 2024
msg:My family traveled and stayed for 2 nights. The package I bought on Ctrip on the first night included breakfast and buffet dinner. It was very cost-effective. It is worth mentioning that the restaurant is located on the top floor, 46th floor, with a good view, especially the night view. The breakfast was quite satisfactory, and everything was available. The dinner was still cost-effective. There were local specialties, puffer fish and freshly fried shellfish. You can choose your favorite small seafood and let the chef fry it. It tasted delicious. There were also curry blue crabs, but they were sold out every time they came out. When it was my turn, there was almost nothing left. The chef was very nice and would specially serve me some from the pot. He was very friendly. Let's talk about the room. We booked a total of 2 business king-size rooms and 1 parent-child room. The business king-size room was upgraded to us on the same day. The parent-child room was very large, especially the bathroom, and the bathtub had a landscape floor-to-ceiling window. Although there were some minor episodes during the few days of stay, the hotel was very active in solving them. I really appreciate their attitude towards dealing with problems, and they are serious and responsible. It is much better than some hotels that only shirk and quibble when encountering problems. The hotel staff also cooperated well with each other and had a strong team spirit. From the lobby manager, restaurant manager, Chinese restaurant service staff, room cleaning aunt, etc., they were all very dedicated. If I have the opportunity to come to Nantong again, I will still choose Vision.

posted:Posted January 28, 2024
msg:I have been staying here. This time I will add a small mistake I made last time.

Last time I said that the small door opposite the charging parking space can lead directly to the hotel lobby. Note that this is only available on weekdays. . On weekends, the connecting door between the office building and the hotel is locked. . It is winter now and it is still a bit cold.

The alternative plan is to enter the office building through the small door (no one is there on weekends but you can enter), take the elevator to the basement, and there is an elevator to the hotel banquet center next to B2, which can go to the lobby on the first floor. . It is five meters apart, but you have to go around once the door on the first floor is locked.
